  <script>
   (function () {

      // Writes meta viewport tags to the page.
      var ua = navigator.userAgent,
          isiPad = ua.match(/iPad/i) != null,
          isiPhone = ua.match(/iPhone/i) != null,
          isiPod = ua.match(/iPod/i) != null,
          isAndroidTablet = ua.match(/Android/i) != null &amp;&amp; !ua.match(/mobile/i),
          isKindle = ua.match(/Kindle/i) != null,
          head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0],
          viewPortTag = document.createElement('meta'),
          meta;

      viewPortTag.name = "viewport";

      // iPhone or iPod
      if (isiPhone || isiPod) {
          viewPortTag.content = "width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0, maximum-scale=1.0, user-scalable=no, minimal-ui";

      // iPad
      } else if (isiPad) {
        viewPortTag.content = "minimal-ui, user-scalable=no";

      // Android
      } else if (isAndroidTablet || isKindle) {

         <p>
          You want to quit anyway, but
          <em>
           make it count.
          </em>
          You want a memorable exit, one that'll go down in history. Like that flight attendant's epic swear-over-the-PA/grab-a-beer/pop-the-emergency-slide resignation
          <a href="http://www.cnn.com/2010/TRAVEL/08/09/new.york.escape.chute.opened/">
           a few years back
          </a>
          . Show up to work wearing an extremely NSFW tee - something that borders on obscenely sexual  for instance. They'll have no choice but to give you the boot on the spot.
         </p>
         <p>
          Let's start with the
          <a href="http://admin.thecrosbypress.com/node/3611925/edit">
           Mighty Healthy Legs Tee
          </a>
          ($29) tee above. Nothing says "I think we're pretty much done here" like rolling into that 9am daily conference call with two glistening, bent-over women emblazoned on your chest.
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="clothing/tees-tanks/4">

          </a>
         </p>
